<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">所以者何？</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　為什麼是這樣呢？</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">巳三、釋2　午一、標生相</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科釋，解釋，分二科；第一科標生相，標出諸行生起的相狀。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">由欲、色、無色界繫法，各從自種子生。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　眾生會得到欲界、色界、或無色界的果報體，都是因為過去栽培了自類界地的種子，果報是從自類的種子所生。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">午二、釋愛因</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科釋愛因，解釋愛是主因。&nbsp;</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">愛名能潤，種是所潤。由此所潤諸種子故，先所牽引各別自體當得生起。如經言：業為感生因，愛為生起因。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　愛名為能滋潤，種子是所滋潤。由於有愛所滋潤的增上緣，使過去所栽培淨不淨業的種子，牽引到淨不淨業所感生的界地受生，三界中各別的自體就可以生起了。如經中說，各式各樣的業，是感得果報生到哪一趣的原因，愛是生起果報的因，也是增上緣。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">巳四、結</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第四科結，結語。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">是故依有潤種子依處，施設生起因。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　因此由前說十五因緣果建立所依處之「有潤種子」依處，安立生起因。生起因的範圍很廣，它通於果報體，也通於心、心所法，及器世間的法。凡是能使法生起的種子，都稱為生起因。例如器世間植物的種子，生芽了，種子相對於芽，種子是芽的生起因。種子生了芽以後會有莖，芽對於莖來說，芽就是種子，莖是由它生起的，所以安立為種子，它是一個安立的法。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">辰五、攝受因4　巳一、標</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第五科攝受因，說明攝受因的所依，分四科；第一科標，標出所依。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">依無間滅因依處，及依境界、根、作用、士用、真實見因依處，施設攝受因。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　依前說建立因緣果的十五種依處中之「無間滅」因依處，及「境界」因依處、「根」因依處、「作用」因依處、「士用」因依處、「真實見」因依處，施設安立攝受因。任何一法的生起，除種子之外的其他一切助緣，都稱為攝受因。無間滅、境界、根、作用、士用，這五種因依處，可以依之建立令有情取得世間法的攝受因；真實見因依處可以依之建立令有情取得無漏的出世間法的攝受因。可以使令有情攝取領受果報的因，稱為攝受因。換句話說，使令有情到三界受生或出離三界所需要各式各樣增上緣，都稱為攝受因。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">巳二、徵</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科徵，提問。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">所以者何？</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　為什麼呢？</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="05p360"></a><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">巳三、釋2　午一、有繫法2　未一、舉欲繫法</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科釋，解釋，分二科；第一科有繫法，有煩惱繫縛的法，又分二科；第一科舉欲繫法，舉出欲界繫法的攝受因。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">由欲繫諸法無間滅攝受故，境界攝受故，根攝受故，作用攝受故，士用攝受故，彼諸行轉。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　在欲界繫的眾生，由自類識開導依的無間滅所攝受使諸識前後相續，加上所緣境、所依根、諸法的作用、與人為的力量，由這種種的助緣攝受而成就欲界諸蘊的生起與活動。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">未二、例色無色繫法</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科例色無色繫法，例舉色無色界繫法的攝受因。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">如欲繫法如是，色無色繫法亦爾。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　如欲繫法如此，色界、無色界的法也一樣，也需要無間滅、境界、根、作用及士用等所攝受，使諸蘊生起活動。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">午二、不繫法</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科不繫法，不繫法的攝受因。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">或由真實見攝受故，餘不繫法轉。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　或由無漏智慧的真實見所攝受，使清淨無漏與聖道相應的不繫法得以設施安立。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">巳四、結</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第四科結，結語。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">是故依無間滅、境界、根、作用、士用、真實見依處，施設攝受因。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　因此依止無間滅、境界、根、作用、士用、真實見，由這六種依止處，能成就諸蘊的生起與活動，而施設為攝受因。所謂攝受因，譬如想種大麥，必須有土地將大麥種在土壤裡面，還需要有肥料、雨水等緣，能夠使令種子生芽，這些助緣都稱為攝受因。有情會生死流轉是因為親近惡知識，聽聞惡法，不如理作意，及種種過去串習的愛及無明煩惱等，這些都是屬於三界流轉生死的攝受因。得到聖道要親近善士、聽聞正法、如理作意、法隨法行，以及精進栽培所修行的信進念定慧，四念處使其能夠成熟，這些都是生起聖道的攝受因。&nbsp;</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》彼諸行轉者：此中彼言，謂欲繫法。於欲繫中色、非色蘊，名彼諸行。隨其所應，依彼依處方能得生，是故說彼依處為攝受因。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　這其中的彼，是指欲界所繫諸法。於欲界繫的色蘊及非色蘊的受想行識，稱為彼諸行。隨其所相應的無間滅依、境界、根、作用、有人的力量等依，諸蘊才能夠生起與活動。色法不用無間滅，只要有種子，有增上緣就能夠生起。因此說彼依處為攝受因。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">辰六、引發因4　巳一、標</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第六科引發因，說明引發因的所依，分四科；第一科標，標出所依。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><a name="3717:3564"></a>依隨順因依處，施設引發因。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　依前說建立因緣果的十五種依處中之「隨順」因依處，安立施設引發因。種子生出現行後，隨順眾緣，前前引發後後而生起下一個結果，依此施設為引發因。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="05p361"></a><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">巳二、徵</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科徵，提問。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">所以者何？</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　怎麼說呢？</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">巳三、釋3　午一、善法4　未一、欲繫2　申一、辨相2　酉一、自增勝</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科釋，解釋，分三科；第一科善法，善法的引發因，又分四科；第一科欲繫，欲界繫眾生善法的引發因，又分二科；第一科辨相，說明引發因的相貌，又分二科；第一科自增勝，引發自地善法增勝。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">由欲繫善法，能引欲繫諸勝善法。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　由欲界繫的善法，能夠引生出欲界更殊勝的善法。例如剛開始做善事時會有些勉強，做久了，善的意樂心逐漸增強，做起來就輕鬆自在，這就是能引諸勝善法。&nbsp;</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">酉二、轉勝上</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科轉勝上，引發展轉殊勝、向上。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">如是欲繫善法，能引色無色繫及不繫善法。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　如前面所說的欲繫善法，能引生出色、無色繫及不繫善法。例如在欲界持戒，依此戒善，修習禪定就可以得到色界，或者無色界定；依止色界定或無色界定，修四念處，修我空觀、法空觀，就可以成就聖道、證得不繫的善法。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">申二、釋因</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科釋因，解釋原因。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">由隨順彼故。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　因為善法是互相隨順的，善法能引生善法。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　在《淨土聖賢錄》裡有一則小小的故事：有一個人不會念佛，也不去念佛，可是他都老是去勸他人去聽淨土的法師講經，勸他人念佛，他這一生勸好多人去念佛。據說他往生時，因為曾勸很多人念佛往生西方，那些往生西方的人很感謝他，就以這個福德因緣，蒙阿彌陀佛來接引他，往生到極樂世界去。開口勸人去念佛這樣小小的善法，就可以得到這麼殊勝的善果。阿難尊者在因地時，行布施飲食幫助沙彌背經，這是欲界善法，後來他就得到陀羅尼，可以過目不忘。所以勿以善小而不為，劣善可以引發勝善，勝善乃至能引發不繫善。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">未二、色繫</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科色繫，色界繫善法的引發因。&nbsp;</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">如欲繫善法，如是色繫善法能引色繫諸勝善法，及無色繫善法、不繫善法。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　如同欲繫善法能引發欲界殊勝的善法，乃至無漏的不繫善法，同樣的色繫善法也能引發色繫更殊勝的善法，及無色界繫善法、乃至無漏的不繫善法。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">未三、無色繫</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科無色繫，無色界繫善法的引發因。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">如色繫善法，如是無色繫善法能引無色繫諸勝善法，及不繫善法。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　如同色繫善法能引發色繫殊勝的善法，乃至無漏的不繫善法，同樣的無色繫善法也能引發無色繫更殊勝的善法，乃至無漏的不繫善法。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　所以佛在《法華經》說：「乃至一低頭皆共成佛道」，由小善能展轉引發大善。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">未四、不繫</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第四科不繫，不繫善法的引發因。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="05p362"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">如無色繫善法，如是不繫善法能引不繫諸勝善法，及能引發無為作證。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　如同無色繫善法能夠引發無色繫的諸勝善法，及不繫善法。無漏的不繫的善法，如戒定慧、三十七道品、四念住，這些不繫的善法，能夠引發不繫的殊勝善法；例如證得初果、二果、三果，展轉的殊勝乃至引發無為作證的涅槃。無為作證，從初果證得我空真如，乃至到四果阿羅漢證得有餘依涅槃，無餘依涅槃，是展轉引發、有次第性的。善法能夠展轉引生殊勝的善法，不論是三界繫或者是不繫法都是一樣。以上是說明善法的引發因。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">午二、不善法2　未一、標</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科不善法，不善法的引發因，分二科；第一科標，標出引發因。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">又不善法能引諸勝不善法。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　又小小的不善法也能夠引發更殊勝、更強有力的不善法。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">未二、釋2　申一、舉欲貪</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科釋，解釋，分二科；第一科舉欲貪，舉欲貪引發各種不善法。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">謂欲貪能引瞋、癡、慢、見、疑、身惡行、語惡行、意惡行。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　欲貪的煩惱能夠引發瞋、癡、慢、見、疑、身惡行、語惡行、意惡行等不善法。欲貪不能滿足時會生起瞋心、欲貪是顛倒錯認所緣境有淨妙相這是一種愚癡，由欲貪所得盛事也能引出高慢心，由欲貪能引發種種邪見、懷疑的煩惱；有了這些煩惱就去造作身惡行、語惡行、意惡行。可見不善法引生更殊勝的不善法，一點點的煩惱就能引生這麼多的罪惡。所謂此有故彼有，真實不虛！</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">申二、例瞋等</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科例瞋等，例瞋等引發不善。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">如欲貪，如是瞋、癡、慢、見、疑，隨其所應盡當知。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　如欲貪煩惱能夠引發其它的煩惱，瞋煩惱、癡煩惱、慢煩惱、見煩惱、疑煩惱也是一樣，隨其所相應的，展轉引發其它的煩惱生起。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">午三、無記法2　未一、辨相2　申一、約種識辨</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科無記法，說明無記法的引發因，分二科；第一科辨相，說明引發因的相貌，又分二科；第一科約種識辨，約種子識說明引發因。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">如是無記法能引善、不善、無記法，如善、不善、無記種子阿賴耶識。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　阿賴耶識是無記法，能夠引生善法、不善法、和無記法。主要是阿賴耶識中有眾多種子，其中善的種子現行成善法，惡的種子現行成不善法，無記法的種子現行成無記法。這是約種子生現行來說明。&nbsp;</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">申二、約段食辨</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科約段食辨，約段食說明引發因。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">又無記法能引無記勝法。如段食能引受生有情令住、令安，勢力增長。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　無記法也能引生無記的勝法。有情所受用的段食可以使令受生有情的色身安住、內心安樂、力量增長，進一步可使有情依持安住的身心修習出世間的聖道。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">未二、釋因</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科釋因，解釋原因。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">由隨順彼故。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　因為隨順身體所需段食的受用，而使無記法的段食發揮它的勝作用。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="05p363"></a><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">巳四、結</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第四科結，結語。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">是故依隨順依處，施設引發因。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　由此依前說十五因緣果建立所依處之「隨順」依處，安立施設引發因。這一法隨順那一法，使這一法能夠引發另一法，施設為引發因。同類有引發因，不同類也可以有引發因；善法可以引發殊勝的善法，不善法可以引發殊勝的不善法。其實不善法也可以引發善法。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　玅境長老喜歡勸居士出家，他曾說了一個例子：某甲的功課成績本來比某乙好，可是某甲很討厭某乙；結果某乙出家修行，有所成就，如此就讓某甲心裡不是滋味，於是某甲也就去出家想要和某乙一樣有成就。其實某甲出家只是基於嫉妒心，卻成就某甲出家的因緣，這是不善法也能引生善法的解釋。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　智者大師說一切惡法都是佛性。我們常說煩惱即菩提，其實在煩惱裡面，只要有智慧一轉，就變成一種逆增上緣，成為成就聖道的因緣，因此有煩惱也不見得是不好，得要看有沒有智慧。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　台灣高雄有位開證長老看到二位出家人吵架，覺得出家人不應該像他們這樣吵架，於是發心復興佛法而出家。有些人看到佛法衰弱，道德淪喪，就想出家修行弘揚佛法，這些人具有慈悲心，有菩薩的種性，就是這種原因。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　證得初地的菩薩，無論什麼法都可以是隨順聖道的，因為他已經有能力往聖道上會。有智慧的人可以轉煩惱，智者轉心不轉境，愚者轉境不轉心。自類善惡法可以展轉引發，他類善惡法也可以因愚智差別而展轉引發。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》如是無記法至阿賴耶識者：阿賴耶識性唯無記，名無記法。彼識中種，有善、不善、無記差別，是故能引善、不善、無記法。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　阿賴耶識性唯是無覆無記，稱為無記法。阿賴耶識的種子有善法、不善、還有無記的差別。這些種子能夠引生善法的現行、不善法的現行、無記法的現行。以種稻子為喻，稻種子生出芽，芽生出來以後能長出莖，莖能長出葉，葉能夠開花，花能夠結果，由種子展轉的相續，相對所結的果來說稱之為引發因。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　三界受生的有情，從無明緣行，乃至取緣有，能夠展轉的前一支引生後一支，後後相續，對望下一生的生老死，稱為引發因；這裡的引發因是指整個的無明乃至有支，造了這個因，就展轉可以引發下一生的生老死，稱為引發因。就清淨的無漏種子所生的一切菩提分法，三十七道品，四念住，四正勤等，能使修行人漸次證得初果乃至有餘依涅槃、無餘依涅槃，這也可稱為引發因。不繫的善法能引發不繫的殊勝善法。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">辰七、定異因4　巳一、標</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第七科定異因，說明定異因的所依，分四科；第一科標，標出所依。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">依差別功能因依處，施設定異因。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　依前說建立因緣果的十五種依處中之「差別功能」因依處，安立施設為定異因。例如造了善法的因，生出來的果一定是善法；造了惡法的因，生出來的果就一定是惡法。不同的因感不同的果，一定不會錯亂的，這是決定不會混亂的定異因。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">巳二、徵</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科徵，提問。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">所以者何？</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　怎麼說呢？</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">巳三、釋2　午一、舉欲繫法</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科釋，解釋，分二科；第一科舉欲繫法，舉出欲繫法的定異因。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">由欲繫諸法自性功能有差別故，能生種種自性功能。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　由於欲界繫諸法的體性功能有差別，因此就能產生種種的自性功能。每一因法有不同，功能也就不同，所引生的果法也就不一樣。色法由色法的種子，心法由心法的種子所生，色心的功能不同，現行的諸法也就不同。因為因不同，果也就不同，由此安立定異因。在〈菩薩地〉卷38，1267頁中說定別因，與定異因文不同義同。如大麥種能生出大麥的芽，它不會產生小麥的芽。看到大麥和小麥，應該知道他們的因不同，大麥種一定是大麥的因，小麥種一定是小麥的因，一定有差別。這就是定別因。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　如果感得投生做人的果報，有屬於人的煩惱和業種子所攝的有支。到地獄去受生的，有地獄的煩惱和業種子所攝的有支。同樣是無明有支十二緣起，人的緣起跟地獄的緣起是不同的，望於五趣的眾生來說，這一些不同的因就稱為定別因。站在果的立場來說，我們投生成為人是因為曾經修持了五戒，感得升為天人則是因為修了十善，墮到地獄去就是因為造了極重的惡業，就果來說因，這是定異因。從果不同就知道因一定有差別，因為它的功能有所不同。如果就清淨法而言，聲聞種姓以聲聞乘能般涅槃，獨覺種姓以獨覺乘能般涅槃，大乘種姓以無上乘能般涅槃，三乘聖道對望所得清淨涅槃為定別因。因不同，所以果不同，稱為定異因。&nbsp;</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">午二、例色繫等法</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科例色繫等法，例色繫等法的定異因。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">如欲繫法，如是色無色繫及不繫法亦爾。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　如同欲界繫法，色界無色界繫的眾生，以及無漏不繫的聖人也都是一樣。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">巳四、結</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第四科結，結語。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="05p364"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">是故依差別功能依處，施設定異因。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　前說十五因緣果建立所依處之「差別功能」依處，施設安立定異因。由於因有差異，果才會有差異。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">辰八、同事因4　巳一、標</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第八科同事因，說明同事因的所依，分四科；第一科標，標出所依。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">依和合因依處，施設同事因。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　依前說建立因緣果的十五種依處中之「和合」因依處，施設同事因。為同一目標，和合共同作一件事，稱為同事因。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">巳二、徵</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科徵，提問。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">所以者何？</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　為什麼呢？</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">巳三、釋2　午一、舉生和合2　未一、舉欲繫法</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科釋，解釋，分二科；第一科舉生和合，舉出生的和合說明同事因，又分二科；第一科舉欲繫法，舉出欲界繫眾生的情況說明同事因。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">要由獲得自生和合故，欲繫法生。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　要由獲得欲界自體受生的種種法和合在一起，才能得到欲界的果報體，使得欲繫法能生起。包括觀待因、牽引因、攝受因、生起因、引發因、定別因，這些種種的因可以總攝為一，稱為同事因。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">未二、例色繫等法</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科例色繫等法，例色繫等法的同事因。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">如欲繫法，如是色無色繫及不繫法亦爾。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　如同欲繫法成就和合一樣，色界或無色界的眾生、聖人，在色界、無色界受生，成就聖道，也有對應自類界地不同的觀待因乃至定異因，由觀待因乃至定別因和合在一起，同做這一件事，而有色無色繫及不繫法生。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">午二、例餘和合</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科例餘和合，例餘和合的同事因。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">如生和合，如是得、成、辦、用和合亦爾。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　如同生的和合，綜合了觀待因、牽引因、攝受因、生起因、引發因、定別因，這些種種的因總攝為一的同事因而成就。「得」，煩惱離繫證得涅槃、「成」就佛法、或者工巧業處能充「辦」等、或是產生作「用」，也是一樣需要各式各樣的因緣和合，才能夠成就。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">巳四、結</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第四科結，結語。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">是故依和合依處，施設同事因。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　所以依止前說十五因緣果建立所依處之「和合」依處，安立施設同事因。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="05p365"></a><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">辰九、相違因4　巳一、標</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第九科相違因，說明相違因的所依，分四科；第一科標，標出所依。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">依障礙因依處，施設相違因。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　依前說建立因緣果的十五種依處中之「障礙」因依處，安立施設相違因。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">巳二、徵</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科徵，提問。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">所以者何？</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　為什麼呢？</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">巳三、釋2　午一、舉生相違2　未一、舉欲繫法</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科釋，解釋，分二科；第一科舉生相違，舉出說明生相違因，又分二科；第一科舉欲繫法，舉出欲繫法說明相違因。&nbsp;</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">由欲繫法將得生，若障礙現前便不得生。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　由於欲界繫法將要得到受生時，如果有障礙的因緣現前，則沒有辦法受生。前面〈意地〉卷1，43頁說欲繫法將得生，需要三處現前，一、其母調適，而復值時；二、父母和合，俱起愛染；三、健達縛正現在前。需此三種條件沒有障礙，才能得生。如果投生時的境界不是自己的父母親，或不是母親排卵時，或者中有沒有現前，或是有其他境界障礙，這些都是有相違因。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">未二、例色繫等法</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科例色繫等法，例說色繫等法的相違因。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">如欲繫法，如是色無色繫及不繫法亦爾。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　如同欲界繫法的生起，如是色無色繫及不繫法也必須沒有障礙。會障礙成就禪定、障礙斷煩惱、障礙開悟的種種因緣，都是相違因。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">午二、例餘相違</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科例餘相違，例說餘相違的相違因。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">如生，如是得、成、辦、用亦爾。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　如同欲界繫法的「生」起必須沒有障礙，同樣的，「得」，煩惱離繫證得涅槃、「成」就佛法、乃至工巧業處充「辦」、業「用」的生起等，也要沒有障礙的相違因，果才能現前。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">巳四、結</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第四科結，結語。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">是故依障礙依處，施設相違因。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　因此依前說十五因緣果建立所依處之「障礙」因依處，安立施設相違因。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">辰十、不相違因4　巳一、標</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第十科不相違因，說明不相違因的所依，分四科；第一科標，標出所依。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="05p366"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">依無障礙因依處，施設不相違因。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　依止前說建立因緣果的十五種依處中之「無障礙」因依處，施設安立不相違因。這是指在得果的過程中沒有障礙作用的因。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">巳二、徵</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科徵，提問。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">所以者何？</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　為什麼？</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">巳三、釋2　午一、舉生不相違2　未一、舉欲繫法</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科釋，解釋，分二科；第一科舉生不相違，舉出生不相違因，又分二科；第一科舉欲繫法，舉出欲界繫法的不相違因。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">由欲繫法將得生，若無障礙現前，爾時便生。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　於欲界繫的果報將生時，如果沒有障礙現前，這時就會成為欲界眾生。又如若此人是念佛的，臨終時沒有人來觸惱障礙他，大家都能幫他助念，使他能保持一心，繫念阿彌陀佛，就可以往生極樂世界。如果此人原是可以往生西方極樂世界，可是臨終前，有逆子出現忤逆他，使他心生懊惱，不但極樂世界去不成，反而可能墮落惡趣。因此種種的緣，對於果來說，不相違因是很重要的。&nbsp;</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">未二、例色繫等法</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科例色繫等法，例色繫等法說明不相違因。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">如欲繫法，如是色無色繫及不繫法亦爾。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　如同欲界繫法的生沒有相違因現前障礙，色界繫法、無色界繫法及無漏的不繫法也是一樣，必須沒有相違因障礙。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">午二、例餘不相違</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科例餘不相違，例說其餘不相違因。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">如生，如是得、成、辦、用亦爾。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　如同生，同樣的，得、成、辦、用各式各樣的果都是一樣，必須沒有相違背的因障礙才能夠成就。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">巳四、結</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第四科結，結語。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">是故依無障礙依處，施設不相違因。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　因此依前說十五因緣果建立所依處之「無障礙」因依處，施設安立不相違因。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　《雜阿含經卷》第39記載，佛陀的弟子，在樹下靜坐忽然生起愛欲心，被佛看到，佛陀對這位比丘說：比丘！比丘！莫種苦種，發熏生臭，惡汁流出。若有比丘種苦種子，發熏生臭，惡汁流出，蛆蠅不集合在此，無有是處！那位比丘就想：『佛已知道我的心念。』於是慚愧恐怖，心驚毛豎，隨路而去。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　有一位比丘聽不懂就請佛陀開示，什麼是苦種？什麼是生臭？什麼是汁流？什麼是蛆蠅？佛陀說：忿怒煩怨名為苦種，五欲功德，名為生臭，於六觸入處不修根律儀，是名汁流，貪、憂、諸惡不善心競生，是名蛆蠅。雖然表面上在靜坐用功，可是不能如理作意，收攝六根，內心生起煩惱，貪著五欲，相違因現前障礙，這樣坐再久也一無是處。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">卯二、四緣4　辰一、因緣</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科四緣，說明四種緣，四緣就是因緣、等無間緣、所緣緣、增上緣，分四科；第一科因緣，說明因緣，一般稱為親因緣。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><a name="40098:3647"></a>復次，依種子緣依處，施設因緣。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　其次，依止種子緣的依處，施設安立因緣。種子緣依處是指前因等十五種依止處的習氣與有潤種子。由所造淨不淨業熏習三界諸行，在阿賴耶識中熏習成習氣種子，淨不淨業是牽引因，牽引有情來生受果報，由於有愛滋潤，使種子達到成熟的階段生起果報，名有潤種子。因緣主要是說種子。在一般的說法中，因與緣是分開的，因是主要條件，緣是次要條件。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="05p367"></a><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">辰二、等無間緣</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科等無間緣，說明四緣中的等無間緣。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">依無間滅緣依處，施設等無間緣。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　依無間滅緣依處，施設等無間緣。無間滅緣依處是指前因等十五種依止處的無間滅因依處。無間滅，指心念的前後相續，自類識前一念滅，是後一念生起的緣，這是心心所法生的條件之一。&nbsp;</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">辰三、所緣緣</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科所緣緣，說明四緣中的所緣緣。所緣緣是心、心所所緣慮的境界。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">依境界緣依處，施設所緣緣。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　依境界緣依處，施設所緣緣。境界緣依處是指前因等十五種依止處的境界因依處。色聲香味觸法，是眼耳鼻舌身意的所緣境。有所緣境，識才能生起。&nbsp;</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">辰四、增上緣</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第四科增上緣，說明四緣中的增上緣。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">依所餘緣依處，施設增上緣。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　依習氣、有潤種子、境界之外所餘緣依處，施設增上緣；或者說，除了因緣等無間緣所緣緣之外的都屬於增上緣，增上緣對果的產生有幫助、加強、成就的作用。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">卯三、五果4　辰一、異熟果及等流果</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科五果，說明五種果，分四科；第一科異熟果及等流果，說明五果中的異熟果及等流果。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">復次依習氣、隨順因緣依處，施設異熟果及等流果。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　其次，依止習氣、隨順因緣依處，施設異熟果及等流果。習氣是指過去所造業行熏為業種形成的牽引因。隨業識經由中陰身入母胎時，其中識、名色、六入、觸、受五法的戲論種子與業種子由愛取滋潤成為有潤種子而現行，就能得到下一世引業所生的異熟果及滿業所生的等流果。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　自類別而言，種子可分二種：一、能產生諸現象（眾生之迷界）者，稱為有漏種子。二、能生菩提之因者，稱為無漏種子。有漏種子又可分為二類：1. 能產生與種子同種類之現象者，稱為名言種子、等流種子、等流習氣。2. 可幫助名言種子，以善惡業而產生異熟作用者（即具有產生當來有漏果之功能），稱為業種子、異熟種子、有支習氣、異熟習氣。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　〈菩薩地〉卷38，1271頁說，「習不善故，樂住不善，不善法增。修習善故，樂住善法，善法增長。或似先業，後果隨轉，是名等流果。」常常修習不善法，於不善法就會增長樂住；常行小的不善，喜歡安住在不善法裡，就有不善法增長，這就是等流果，所種的因與所得的果是平等的，果是因的平等流類。前生喜歡瞋，常常生氣，形成了習慣，下一念碰到類似境界還是會生氣，這是等流果。略說異熟果和等流果的分別，若感得五趣或做人的果報體，這是異熟果；所說的話他人都常不相信，這是宿生有妄語的習性所感得的等流果；過去生常有殺生這一生就是多病，這也是屬於等流果。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》依習氣隨順因緣依處等者：習氣依處為牽引因，即種子緣所依；隨順依處為引發因，即增上緣所依；是名習氣、隨順因緣依處。依牽引因及種子緣，施設異熟果。依引發因及增上緣，施設等流果。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　依習氣依處施設牽引因，也就是種子緣建立的依止處；依隨順依處施設引發因，也就是增上緣建立的所依處，是名習氣、隨順因緣依處。依止過去業行成就的牽引因及種子緣，施設為異熟果。依止引發因及增上緣，而施設安立等流果。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">辰二、離繫果</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科離繫果，說明五果中的離繫果。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">依真實見因緣依處，施設離繫果。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　依真實見因緣依處，施設安立離繫果。十五種因等依處中第十個真實見，就是無漏的智慧，有無漏的智慧才能證果。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="05p368"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》依真實見因緣依處施設離繫果者：此中因緣，謂攝受因及增上緣。如是因緣依真實見，名真實見因緣依處。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　此處因緣，是指攝受因及增上緣。以上因緣，以真實見作為依止，稱為真實見因緣依處。無間滅、境界、根、作用、士用、真實見等依處，在十種因中屬於攝受因，真實見依處在四種緣中屬於增上緣，依止攝受因與增上緣，安立離繫果。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">辰三、士用果</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科士用果，說明五果中的士用果。&nbsp;</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">依士用因緣依處，施設士用果。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　依前說的士用因緣依處，施設安立士用果。士用就是人為的力量，從事士農工商等行業的人，依工巧智慧、輔以工具，所成就的結果，都是士用果。例如農夫的莊稼有收成；商人的貨流往來賺錢；工巧業處的工巧智慧發生作用與建設；教書能作育英才，有人有法，這些都是士用果。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》依士用因緣依處施設士用果者：此中因緣，如前真實見因緣依處釋。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　這其中的士用因緣，如同前面真實見因緣依處的解釋，無間滅、境界、根、作用、士用等為攝受因，士用因緣依處於四緣中屬於增上緣，依止攝受因與增上緣，安立士用果。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">辰四、增上果</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第四科增上果，說明五果中的增上果。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">依所餘因緣依處，施設增上果。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　依其他所餘因緣依處，施設安立為增上果。每一法有每一法的作用，色法有色法的作用，心法有心法的作用，地水火風各有各的不同作用，這些都是屬於依作用依處建立的增上果。例如眼識就是眼根的增上果，依眼根緣境，能夠發出眼識。眾生的身體能夠維持，是命根的增上果，有命根能使令生命不壞。二十二根中各有各的增上果，各各不同。以上是約依止處與因緣果的關係，建立因緣果的說明。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">寅二、辨義相2　卯一、釋三義</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科辨義相，說明建立因緣果的義相，分二科；第一科釋三義，解釋因緣果的義相。這是以另一個角度說明成就因、緣、果的三種義相。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><a name="11360:3668"></a><a name="28652:3668"></a><a name="3436:3668"></a>復次，順益義是因義，建立義是緣義，成辦義是果義。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　其次，順益義是指種子的因義，建立義是使法能生起的緣義，成辦義是使果能成就的果義。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">卯二、辨因相2　辰一、五種相2　巳一、約法體辨2　午一、標列</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科辨因相，詳細說明因的義相，分二科；第一科五種相，將十種因又歸納成五種相貌，又分二科；第一科約法體辦，約法體說明因相，又分二科；第一科標列，標示列出五相。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">又建立因有五種相。一、能生因，二、方便因，三、俱有因，四、無間滅因，五、久遠滅因。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　又從法體的角度說，建立因有能生因、方便因、俱有因、無間滅因、久遠滅因的五種相。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">午二、隨釋5　未一、能生因</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科隨釋，接著解釋，分五科；第一科能生因，說明能生因的義相。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="05p369"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">能生因者，謂生起因。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　能生因，就是生起因，能生起各式各樣的法。有潤種子能生出生命體，如由欲、色、無色界繫法，各從自種子生。如經所說：業是感生因，愛是生起因、也是增上緣。因此依有潤種子依止處，施設安立生起因。即各個種子，對望所成就的自體果，名為生起因。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">未二、方便因</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科方便因，說明方便因的義相。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">方便因者，謂所餘因。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　除了生起因以外，其他的九種因都稱為方便因。方便有隨順、幫助的意思，可以幫助成就果法生起。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">未三、俱有因2　申一、明一分</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科俱有因，說明俱有因的義相，分二科；第一科明一分，說明攝受因一分是俱有因。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">俱有因者，謂攝受因一分。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　俱有因，是攝受因的一部分。攝受因的建立包括無間滅、境界、根、作用、士用、真實見等依處。根，是其中一部分。〈五識身相應地〉中說到所依，包括俱有依、等無間依、種子依。眼識的俱有依是眼根，依根緣境生識。俱有因，是指同時存在的因，例如任何色法都是四大組成的，所以於色法中四大是俱有因。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">申二、舉眼等</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科舉眼等，舉眼識等說明俱有因。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">如眼於眼識，如是耳等於所餘識。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　如眼根對於眼識是眼識的俱有因，耳根相對於耳識，鼻根相對於鼻識，乃至意根相對於意識，都是自類根的俱有因，而根是攝受因中的一部分。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">未四、無間滅因</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第四科無間滅因，說明無間滅因的義相。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">無間滅因者，謂生起因。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　無間滅因就是生起因，生起因就前面來說，是指有潤種子，換句話說，前念滅後無間引得後生之有潤種子可稱為生起因。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">未五、久遠滅因</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第五科久遠滅因，說明牽引因的義相。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">久遠滅因者，謂牽引因。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　久遠滅因是久遠所造的業行已滅了，但是所造業行同時熏成業種，此業種在未來會牽引感得後世的果報，這類種子稱為牽引因。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="05p370"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》無間滅因至牽引因者：於前自體無間滅已，後之自體無間得生。於爾所時，愛所潤種為新生因，是名無間滅因。淨不淨業既造作已，雖久遠滅，然有彼種而不捨離，依自相續而得生起，是名久遠滅因。又緣起支次第相望，皆有無間滅及久遠滅二種緣義，如下當說。（<a href="http://mahabodhi.org/yoga/cb/10.htm#3685:7578">陵本十卷九頁772</a>）</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　阿賴耶識種子剎那生滅相續不己，前自體滅後得無間引生後自體。為此「滅後無間能生」所攝受，依有潤種子建立新生因，是名無間滅因。善不善業雖已造作，久遠謝滅，在造作時同時熏成業種，隨阿賴耶識自體相續，遇緣得以現行引生異熟果，是名久遠滅因。又依十二緣起前後支的次第相望，前支是後支生起的緣，都有無間滅及久遠滅二種的緣義。在〈有尋有伺等三地〉卷10，322頁的地方還會再說。這是約十種因的法體來說。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">巳二、約業用辨2　午一、標</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科約業用辨，由業用說明因緣果的義相，分二科；第一科標，標示出五相。&nbsp;</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">又建立因有五種相。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　建立因約業用來說，又有五種相貌。&nbsp;</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">午二、列</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科列，列出五相。&nbsp;</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">一、可愛因，二、不可愛因，三、增長因，四、流轉因，五、還滅因。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　將十種因，約能產生果報的不同，歸納成五種。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　一、可愛因：造作得到人天果報的因。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　二、不可愛因：造作感得三惡道的因。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　三、增長因：有助於因能達到果的力量。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　四、流轉因：世間可愛因的善法、不可愛因的不善法、及增長因，由於沒有究竟斷除煩惱，最後的果報都是流轉生死。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　五、還滅因：依真實見依處，修無漏的善法斷除煩惱，不再流轉生死。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">辰二、七種相3　巳一、標</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科七種相，說明建立因的七種義相，分三科；第一科標，標出七相，建立因的七種相與《攝大乘論》中的種子六義，或是與《成唯識論》的種子六義是相通的。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">又建立因有七種相。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　又建立因有七種相貌。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">巳二、釋7　午一、要是無常</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科釋，解釋，分七科；第一科要是無常，要是無常才能為因。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">謂無常法是因，無有常法能為法因。謂或為生因，或為得因，或為成立因，或為成辦因，或為作用因。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　建立有為法，它的因必須是無常法，不是常法能為因。如果是常住不變的事物就沒有所謂的因果了，一定會改變才會使因得果，因此無常法才能夠做為有為法的因。這些無常的法或是能使果法生起的因，或是能使果法得到的因，或是能使果法成立的因，或是能使果法成辦的因，或是能使果法生起作用的因。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="05p371"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》無常法是因等者：若法有生滅，是名無常法；若法無生滅，是即名常法。由無常法有生滅故，業用可得，故能為因。常法不爾，故說非因。此中為因說有五種，十因差別隨應當知。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　法要是有生有滅，名為無常法。法如果是常住不變，沒有生滅的就名為常法。因為無常法有生有滅，明顯的可以看到它有作用，因此能夠為因。常住不變的常法，就不能稱之為因，因為它一直都沒有改變。這裡說有生因，得因，成立因，成辦因，作用因五種是約前面生、得、成、辦、用這五種果來說的。十種因的差別隨所相應的，應當知道。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">午二、要望他性及後自性2　未一、標二種</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科要望他性及後自性，要望他性及後自性能為因相，分二科；第一科標二種，標出二種。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">又雖無常法為無常法因，然與他性為因，亦與後自性為因。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　又雖然是無常法為無常法的因，然而是與所生不同體性的果為因，也與自相續的後一剎那生起的自果為因。當種生現，現生種，種現三法同時，種子是因、現行是果，種子與現行是同時的，名為與他性為因。當種子未遇緣，隨阿賴耶識自相續時，在剎那生滅中，前一剎那滅是後一剎那生起的因，這是異時因果名為與後自性為因。由於無常變異，果和因是不同的。例如眼識的種子產生現行，眼識就有了別色塵的功能，種子與現行的體性不同稱為他，此時眼識種子稱為與他性為因；當眼識尚未現行，在阿賴耶識中剎那剎那前後相續，此時眼識種子稱為與後自性為因。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">未二、隨難釋</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科隨難釋，隨著解釋較難懂的部分。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">非即此剎那。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　與後自性為因，種子生種子，不是同時因果，是異時因果。同類的種子，自相續前一剎那滅後一剎那生，前後剎那不是同時的因果，是異時的因果。前一剎那與後一剎那種子自性是一樣的，因此說亦以後自性為因。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》然與他性為因等者：種生現行，名與他性為因；果望於因，性非是一，故名為他。種生自種，名與自性為因；種望於種，因性是一，故名為自。若與他性為因，當知同一剎那；若與自性為因，當知非一剎那。為顯此義，故說後言。種安住位，因性隨轉，恆相續故。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　種子生現行，稱為與他性為因，種子是因、現行是果，現行的果對望種子的因，體性並不是一樣的，因此名為他。種子隨阿賴耶識自相續時自種能生自種子，稱為與自性為因，種子對於自種，都還沒有現行，同樣是現行法的因，因性方面是一樣的，所以名為自。若是作為體性不同的果的因，應當知道是同一剎那，就是同時因果；如果是與種子自相續的自性為因，應知不是同一剎那，而是前後剎那。為了顯示其中前後因果的義理，所以稱為後。種子處於安住的狀態，它的因性隨著阿賴耶識的相續，隨逐而轉，恆常相續。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">午三、要已生未滅</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科要已生未滅，要已生未滅才是因相。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">又雖與他性為因，及與後自性為因，然已生未滅方能為因，非未生已滅。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　種子因對望於現行果，是不同的體性，因此是與他性為因；種子的自相續，前一剎那滅後一剎那生，能與後自性為因，然而這二種情況都是要種子已生未滅，才能作為因，並不是尚未生起或是已經謝滅的情形。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》然已生未滅等者：已生未滅相是現在，未生相是未來，已滅相是過去。如前意地已說。（<a href="http://mahabodhi.org/yoga/cb/03.htm#3703:2065">陵本三卷七頁221</a>）今應準釋。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　已生未滅相是指現在，未生相是指未來，已滅相是指過去。種子必須是在現前，現前才能夠成為後自性的因，及與他性為因。如〈意地〉卷3，95頁所說，現在應準照〈意地〉所說解釋。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="05p372"></a><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">午四、要得餘緣</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第四科要得餘緣，要得餘緣才能為因相，這是指要待眾緣。&nbsp;</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">又雖已生未滅，然得餘緣方能為因，非不得餘緣。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　又因已種下去了，雖然已生未滅，現在種子已存在，可是要有使它生起的緣才能夠為因。因為它成為果了才稱為因，如沒有其它的助緣，果不現行不能夠成為因。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》然得餘緣等者：謂彼彼行生緣現前，彼彼行因生彼彼行，非不待緣諸行得生。由是道理，諸行雖有各別生因，而無俱時頓生起過。如下決擇分說。（<a href="http://mahabodhi.org/yoga/cb/51.htm#3707:39896">陵本五十一卷十六頁4122</a>）</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　各式各樣有為法的因，有生起的緣現前，才能夠產生各式各樣的有為法，有了種子因，還要有其它的緣，諸行才能得生，並不是沒有待眾緣而能夠生出種種的現行法。心心所法生要四緣具足，色法要因緣與增上緣二種緣。每一法有每一法的緣，緣具足不具足有差別。阿賴耶識雖然有三界的種子，因為各個種子都要待眾緣，所以沒有俱時頓然生起的過失。如〈決擇‧五識身相應地意地〉卷51，1710頁所說。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">午五、要成變異</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第五科要成變異，要成變異才能為因相。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">又雖得餘緣，然成變異方能為因，非未成變異。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　又雖然因得到了其他的緣，然而要經過變異成熟才能成為因，並不是沒有變異成熟能成為因，變異才能成熟。種子栽培下去，還要待其成熟，才能夠發芽。例如靜坐得禪定，必須要經過長時間的練習、栽培熏習，才能得定。所以雖然待眾緣，可是種子也要變異，種子要變異成熟才能成為法的因。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》然成變異等者：種若成熟，是名變異。生緣攝受，異前相故。</span></strong></span></span></p>
