<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　另一種解釋，修禪定，首先要持戒清淨，與大眾利合同均，共同受用如法追求的衣服飲食坐臥具等，名引攝資生具；引攝有喜樂是指初禪和二禪；引攝離喜樂是指第三禪，因為第三禪是離喜的樂。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　這二種解釋，以前一種的解釋範圍比較廣些。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="05p387"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》復有三種引攝等者：如法追求衣服、飲食、諸坐臥具、病緣醫藥、資身什物，與眾同用，是名引攝資生具。善能教授教誡，令證瑜伽作意止觀，隨其所應，當知引攝有喜樂及離喜樂。謂初二靜慮名有喜樂，第三靜慮名離喜樂。或前三靜慮有喜及樂，名有喜樂；第四靜慮以上諸定離喜及樂，名離喜樂。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　佛陀說在家眾出家眾如法追求衣服、飲食、種種的坐臥具，病緣醫藥資生雜物，得到後，要與大眾共同受用，這是引攝資生具。大家共住在一起，善知識能夠教授修定修慧的方法，教導如何持守戒律；教導訓誡什麼是不可以做，什麼是可以做，使令能夠證得瑜伽相應作意的止觀，隨其所相應的，引生得到有喜樂及離喜樂的境界。初二靜慮名為有喜樂，第三靜慮名為離喜樂，這是第一種解釋。或者說得到初禪、二禪有喜，三禪有樂，名有喜樂；第四禪以上都是捨受，喜受樂受也沒有了，稱為離喜樂。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">子二、隨轉供事3　丑一、標列種類</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科隨轉供事，恆順眾生、供養承事眾生的如理作意，分三科；第一科標列種類，標示列出四種。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">復有四種隨轉供事。一、隨轉供事非知舊者，二、隨轉供事諸親友者，三、隨轉供事所尊重者，四、隨轉供事具福慧者。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　又有四種隨順眾生的需要承事供養他們的事：</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　一、隨轉供事非知舊者：不認識的人，而且也不是自己的朋友，能夠供養他。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　二、隨轉供事諸親友者：自己的親戚、朋友、父母這些親人，能隨其心意去供養。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　三、隨轉供事所尊重者：自己所尊敬的師長或其他的同參道友，能隨對方的心意去供養承事。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　四、隨轉供事具福慧者：在周圍中有大福報大智慧的人，也能夠隨順對方的心意去供養承事。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">丑二、明彼果利2　寅一、總標</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科明彼果利，說明供養承事的果報利益，分二科；第一科總標，總相標出果報利益。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">由此四種隨轉供事，依止四處，獲得五果應知。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　這四種恆順眾生，供養承事的事情，依止四種處所，可以獲得五種殊勝的果報。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">寅二、別釋2　卯一、依處2　辰一、徵</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科別釋，一一作各別解釋四種依處及五種果，分二科；第一科依處，先說明依處，又分二科；第一科，問。&nbsp;</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">何等四處？</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　是哪四種依處呢？</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">辰二、列</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科列，列出四種依處。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">一、無攝受處，二、無侵惱處，三、應供養處，四、同分隨轉處。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　分別標示出來隨轉供事對象的四種依處。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　一、無攝受處：供養不認識的對象。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　二、無侵惱處：親友都是和合的，不會互相侵惱。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　三、應供養處：自己所尊重的人是應該供養的。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　四、同分隨轉處：同樣具福慧的人，與自己共住在一起的同修梵行者，能承事供養他。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="05p388"></a><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">卯二、得果2　辰一、標</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科得果，得到五種果，分二科；第一科標，標出所得果。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">依此四處，能感五果。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　在這四種處所，無攝受處、無侵惱處、應供養處、同分隨轉處若能承事供養，能感得五種果報。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">辰二、列</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科列，列出五種。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">一、感大財富，二、名稱普聞，三、離諸煩惱，四、證得涅槃，五、或往善趣。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　依這四種處所去承事供養，隨順眾生，能感得下列五種果報。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　一、感得大財富：因為供養有福慧功德的人，會感得大財富。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　二、名稱普聞：由於內心調柔，有忍辱心，因此名聲遠揚各地。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　三、離諸煩惱：於煩惱起厭離心而離欲，能夠遠離煩惱。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　四、證得涅槃：作了種種承事供養的事，有了福報，修離欲、斷煩惱，能夠證得三乘涅槃：聲聞乘、緣覺乘的有餘依或無餘依涅槃、或是佛菩薩的無住大般涅槃。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　五、或往善趣：如果不想涅槃，只是修五戒十善，能投生到人天的善趣。依止四處，供養承事有這五種好處。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》無攝受處者：由非知舊不為自所攝受故，名無攝受處。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　因為所攝受的對象不是過去認識的，也不是自己所攝受的，名為無攝受處。以上是說到隨轉供事，可見佛教對這件事也很重視。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">丑三、釋具慧相2　寅一、依三慧辨</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科釋具慧相，解釋具足智慧的相貌，分二科；第一科依三慧辨，依聞思修三種智慧說明具慧相。&nbsp;</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">又聰慧者有三種聰慧相。一、於善受行，二、於善決定，三、於善堅固。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　又聰明有智慧的人，有三種相貌。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　一、於善受行：這是屬於聞慧的範圍；這種人於佛法能夠善於聽聞領受。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　二、於善決定：這是屬於思慧的範圍。接受善法之後，能用清淨心去思惟、籌量、觀察、簡擇，因此對善法有決定的信心。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　三、於善堅固：這是屬於修慧的範圍。有修慧的人因為有修行，在未到地定裡面修四念處，或者修無我觀等，對於所聽聞的法，能深入思惟簡擇，恆常串習修行，使善法堅固。&nbsp;</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》又聰慧者有三種聰慧相等者：由聞慧故，聞正法已，信受奉行，是名於善受行。由思慧故，於所聞法清淨思惟、籌量、觀察，是名於善決定。由修慧故，於所聞思住念正知，是名於善堅固。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　於善受行是由於聞慧，聽聞了正法以後，能信受奉行，名為於善受行。由於有思惟的智慧，對於所聽聞的法，能夠以清淨心，就是沒有染污的心，思惟、籌量、觀察，名為於善決定。由於有修慧，智慧增長了，令心安住在聞思所決擇的正念上，更以正知堅固之，名為於善堅固。&nbsp;</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">寅二、依三學辨</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科依三學辨，依三學說明具慧相。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">復有三相。一、受學增上戒，二、受學增上心，三、受學增上慧。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　尚有三種相，受學增上戒、受學增上心、受學增上慧。受學是信受學習，從增上戒、增上心、增上慧，這三個相貌來說明。增上有二義，一是所趣義，是往那裡去，可以使令達到更高的境界；另一義是最勝義，它是不共外道的。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　一、受學增上戒：受學的戒是清淨的，依止戒可以得定，戒有增上定的作用。佛法裡的戒也是不共外道的，是最殊勝的，沒有我的執著，沒有戒禁取的執著。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　二、受學增上心：受學增上心的人，也是有智慧的人，依止禪定，能夠得到世間的智慧乃至出世間的智慧。佛法中的禪定沒有執著，也是最殊勝的。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　三、受學增上慧：以增上心為依止，可以得到智慧，這種智慧通於調伏煩惱的世間智與斷除煩惱的出世間智。剛開始時，還沒有得到出世間智，但至少能夠遠離欲，以所修習得到的慧，再以此為基礎，能夠增上證得無漏的聖道，增上慧也是不共外道的智慧。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　若能受學增上戒、增上心、及增上慧，就是一位有智慧的人。&nbsp;</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="05p389"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》復有三相等者：一切諸學，三學所攝。謂戒、心、慧。由所趣義及最勝義，名為增上。如下聲聞地釋。（<a href="http://mahabodhi.org/yoga/cb/28.htm#3856:23216">陵本二十八卷二頁2329</a>）思所成地引伽他言：最先離惡作，最後樂成滿，初學是為初，於此學聰叡。由此智修淨，淨生樂成滿，諸學是為中，於此學聰叡。從此心解脫，永滅諸戲論，諸學是為尊，於此學聰叡。（<a href="http://mahabodhi.org/yoga/cb/16.htm#3856:13927">陵本十六卷十六頁1424</a>）依此當知三聰慧相。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　佛法的一切學問裡面，由戒、心、慧三種學所涵蓋，戒心慧就是戒定慧。如前說增上有二義，一是所趣義，二是最勝義，如下〈聲聞地〉卷28，940頁所說。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　約所趣義說：為趣增上心修淨戒名增上戒學。持戒是為得到定，增上心是以修淨戒為基礎，由持戒不做惡事、無悔、歡喜、心安，戒清淨能夠得定。為趣增上慧而修定，希望得到智慧而修定，稱為增上心學。為趣煩惱斷而修智見，名為增上慧學。慧就是思惟觀察，為能夠斷除煩惱，必須修學智慧和正見，稱為增上慧學。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　約最勝義說：唯獨佛教有的戒定慧，是不共外道的。外道也有戒定慧，但不是增上的戒、定、慧，外道有的是邪見，佛教有的才是不共外道的正見，因此是最勝義。〈思所成地〉卷16引偈頌說明增上戒、增上心、增上慧三學：「最先離惡作，最後樂成滿，初學是為初，於此學聰叡。」由於持戒清淨而不犯錯，遠離惡作而無悔，無悔則歡悅，由歡悅而心喜，由心喜能令身安、身安故而成滿受樂得定。在三學中最初開始要學習的是增上戒，戒是最基礎，由學戒、領受戒、執持戒，修戒清淨，由此能引發聰叡通達實相。這句是顯示由增上戒學，以無悔等漸次修習為後來成就聰叡的因。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　「由此智修淨，淨生樂成滿，諸學是為中，於此學聰叡。」由心得正定，能如實知見，能起厭離世間的觀慧因此遠離三界欲染，由離三界欲染故得解脫，得解脫故證無所作究竟涅槃。這句是顯示由增上心學，修所成慧最勝善根漸次而生，是最上學的因。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　「從此心解脫，永滅諸戲論，諸學是為尊，於此學聰叡。」於有餘依涅槃位中，愛見煩惱種子滅除，煩惱永斷，名心解脫。若入無餘依涅槃界，一切我與身若異不異，死後當有或當無等戲論不能說故，名永滅戲論。戒定慧這三學，是佛所說的內容，在三學的內容裡面，學習到了聰明睿智的智慧，使令心能夠解脫，永久滅除種種分別的名言戲論。這句是顯示由增上慧學，能為最勝涅槃果的因。如〈思所成地〉卷16，604～605頁所說，這是有聰明智慧者具有三種智慧的相貌。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　以上是如理作意施設建立，以偈頌：「依處及與事，求受用正行，二菩提資糧，到彼岸方便」詳細說明由依處故、事故、求故、受用故、正行故、聲聞乘資糧方便故、獨覺乘資糧方便故、波羅蜜多引發方便故等八種相貌。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">瑜伽師地論科句披尋記卷第五</span></strong></span></span></p>
